<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> 12. MAJOR CUSTOMERS  </B></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Sales to one customer comprised approximately 52% of net sales for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2009, and sales to two customers comprised 48% and 10% for the year ended
December&nbsp;31, 2008, respectively. Amounts due from the one customer in 2009 and the two customers in 2008 comprised approximately 50% and 63% of trade receivables at December&nbsp;31, 2009 and
2008, respectively. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> 13. COMMITMENTS AND CONTINGENCIES  </B></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> Royalty Commitments  </I></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Summer Infant (USA), Inc has entered into various license agreements with third parties for the use of product designs and trade names
for the products manufactured by the Company. These agreements have termination dates through August, 2013. Royalty expense under these licensing agreements for the years ended December&nbsp;31,
2009 and 2008 were approximately $910,000 and $214,000, respectively. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> Customer Agreements  </I></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company enters into annual agreements with its customers in the normal course of business. These agreements define the terms of
product sales including in some instances cooperative advertising costs and product return privileges (for defective products only) or defective allowances (which are based upon historical
experience). These contracts are generally annual in nature and obligate the Company only as to products actually sold to the customer. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> License Agreements and Lease Commitments  </I></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Summer USA leases an office under a three-year agreement which requires monthly payments of approximately $3,000 through
September 2010. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Summer
USA leases certain vehicles under non-cancelable operating lease agreements. These leases are for a three-year term requiring monthly payments of
approximately $8,000 through November 2012. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Summer
USA leases an office under a four year agreement which requires monthly payments of approximately $3,400 through July 2012. </FONT></P>


<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SIE
leases office space under a non-cancelable operating lease agreement. This lease is for a five-year term through April 2012, and requires monthly payments of
approximately $6,500. In addition, SIE is required to pay its proportionate share of property taxes. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Summer
Infant Canada,&nbsp;Ltd. entered into a five-year lease for office and warehouse space under a non-cancelable operating lease agreement expiring March
2013. The Company is obligated as part of the lease to pay maintenance expenses as well as property taxes and insurance costs as defined in the agreement. Monthly payments for the initial year are
approximately $13,000 and escalate over the course of the lease term. Summer Infant Canada&nbsp;Ltd. has the option to renew this lease for one additional period of five years under the same terms
and conditions. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Summer
Infant (USA)&nbsp;Inc. entered into a 28&nbsp;month lease for office and warehouse space under a non-cancelable operating lease agreement. The Company is obligated
to pay certain common area maintenance charges including insurance and utilities. Monthly payments for the initial year are approximately $29,750 and escalate over the course of the lease term. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>F-24</FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> Employment Contracts  </I></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In accordance with United Kingdom and EU law, SIE has employment contracts with all employees. In connection with these contracts, SIE
is required to fund the individual pension contributions of certain employees at varying rates from 5% to 10% of the employee's annual salary, as part of their total compensation package. These
pension contributions are expensed as incurred. There are no termination benefit provisions in these contracts. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> Factoring Agreement  </I></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In 2009 SIE entered into an accounts receivable factoring agreement with Coface. SIE receives advances from Coface based on actual
accounts receivable created by SIE. The total advances outstanding as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 totaled approximately $472,000, which is recorded as a current liability. </FONT></P>


<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I> Litigation  </I></FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company is involved in various claims and legal actions arising in the ordinary course of business. Management is of the opinion
that the ultimate outcome of these matters would not have a material adverse impact on the financial position of the Company or the results of its operations. </FONT></P>
